 Aajtak's team found that at present, most of the crop in Punjab is ready to be harvested and only 10% of the crop has been harvested, that too of early maturing paddy varieties
 haalanki punjab or haryana main abhi kisaanon ne zyada paraali nahin jalaai he, lekin har gaanv main paraali jalaane ke ikkaa-dukka maamle jarur saamne aa rahe hai

 Pakistan is also polluting Delhi

 is chitthee main sunil aroda ne likhaa tha ki ek khaas company ko phayda pahunchane ke liye prafull patel ne jarurat se zyada jet plane kharidwaye
 Indian Airlines are not allowed to fly on profitable routes
 jaahir he, is maamle par vipaksh ne hallaa shuru kar diya he
 Prabodh Panda of CPI and Nishikant Dubey of BJP have demanded a CVC inquiry
 royles ne ajinkya rahane (74) or captain shen watasan (45) kii umdaa pariyon kii madad se chah wicket par 191 ran banaae jiske baad kings ilevan punjab ne bhi shaun marsh (65) or david miller (54) ke ardhashtakon kii madad se yahi score khadaa kiya
 In the super over, Punjab gave the Royals a target of 16 runs but the team lost both their wickets for six runs off the first three balls
 super over main punjab kii team pehle ballebaaji karne utari
 Marsh and Miller were once again on the field while the ball was in the hands of Chris Maurice
 mauris ne pehali hi gend phultos phenki or miller chookkar pagabaadha out ho gaye
 Glenn Maxwell took one run off the second ball
 marsh ne iske baad lagaataar teen chauke maare jisamen nobal par chaukaa bhi shaamil rahaa
 The next ball went empty while one run scored on the last ball, giving the Royals a target of 16 runs
 royles kii ore se watasan or james foconor pehle utre jabaki gend mishael johnson ne thami
 Johnson bowled Watson on the first ball
 steven smith ne agali nobal par chaukaa maaraa
 One run scored on the next ball
 foconor iske baad agali gend ko chook gaye or krij se baahar nikal aae jiske baad wicketiper riddhimaan saaha ne unhen stump karke punjab ko duusari jeet dilaai
 The Royals' team became part of the tie match for the third time and they had to face defeat after winning the last two times
 royles kii chah maichon main yah pehali haar he or vah ab bhi 10 ank ke saath sheersh par he
 The Punjab team has four points from five matches
 punjab kii shuruuaat kharaab rahi
 The team lost the wicket of Virender Sehwag (01) in the second over, who was leading the team in place of George Bailey
 vah smith ke stick nishane kaa shikaar bane
 Opener Murali Vijay (21) hit a six off Stuart Binny but he was lucky when Karun Nair was caught by a proficient copper ball
 vijay ne iske baad mauris par bhi chakka jadaa lekin vah ran out hokar pavilion laute
 Marsh, who was playing the first match of the tournament, meanwhile played some exciting shots
 binni or tambe par chauke jadne ke baad unhone rahul tevatiya par bhi do chauke maare
 Maxwell (01) however failed once again and was caught by Smith at deep midwicket off leg-spinner Teotia, leaving Punjab at 59 for three
 marsh ne tevatiya par do chhakkon ke saath 32 gend main ardhashatak puraa kiya
 Miller completed the team's century in the 13th over with a six over Watson
 marsh haalanki tambe par chakka jadne kii koshish main long on par rahane ko kaich de baithe jisase miller ke saath unki 58 ran kii tufaani saajhedaari kaa ant hua
 Marsh faced five fours and three sixes in 40 balls
 punjab ko antim paanch over main jeet ke liye 72 ran kii darkaar thi
 Miller increased the run pace with two consecutive sixes over Faulkner
 riddhimaan saaha (8 gend main 19 ran) ne bhi mauris par teen chauke jade lekin is tej gendbaaj kii sidhi gend ko chookkar bold ho gaye
 Miller completed 50 off 29 balls with two sixes over Hooda but caught Binny off the next ball
 unhone 30 gend kii apni pari main ek chaukaa or paanch chakke maare
 Earlier Rahane added 95 runs for the first wicket with captain Watson laying the foundation for the team's strong score
 unhone deepak hooda (19) ke saath duusare wicket ke liye sirf 3
 Also added 41 runs in 3 overs
 orange cap dharak rahane shuru se hi lay main najar aae
 He hit two fours in two consecutive overs of Mitchell Johnson after hitting a four off Sandeep Sharma
 watasan ne bhi anurit singh par chaukaa jadaa
 The Royals scored 43 runs in six overs of the power play
 watasan ne iske baad morcha sambhala
 He hit three fours and a six off off-spinner Shivam Sharma's successive balls, while Akshar Patel also hit a six off the long off
 akshar ne watasan ko riddhimaan saaha ke haathon stump karake royles ko pehla jhatka diya
 Watson hit five fours and two sixes in his 35-ball innings
 tippaniyan Rahane completed the hundred of the team's runs in the 12th over with a single off Glenn Maxwell, while Hooda hit two sixes in the same over
 rahane ne agle over main anurit par deep midwicket ke upar se chakka jadkar 40 gend main lagaataar teesraa ardhashatak puraa kiya
 Rahane also hit Shivam for a six but the off-spinner bowled Hooda
 hooda ne nau gend main ek chaukaa or do chakke maare

 Punjab's team came out to bat first in the Super Over
 marsh or miller kii jodi ek baar phir maidan par thi jabaki gend kris mauris ke haath main thi
 Maurice bowled a full ball first and Miller missed out lbw
 glen maxwell ne duusari gend par ek ran liya
 Marsh then hit three consecutive fours, including a four at Nobol
 agali gend khaali gai jabaki antim gend par ek ran bana jisase royles ko 16 ran kaa lakshya mila
 Watson and James Faulkner landed first for the Royals while Mitchell Johnson held the ball
 johnson ne pehali hi gend par watasan ko bold kiya
 Steven Smith next hit Noble
 agali gend par ek ran bana
 Faulkner then missed the next ball and came out of the crease after which wicketkeeper Wriddhiman Saha stumped him to give Punjab a second win
 royles kii team teesri baar taai match kaa hissaa bani or pichhali do baar jeetne ke baad is baar use haar jhelni padi
 This is the Royals' first defeat in six matches and is still on top with 10 points
 punjab kii team ke paanch maichon main chaar ank hai
 Punjab started poorly
 team ne duusare over main hi virendra sahvaag (01) kaa wicket ganvaa diya jo jorge baili kii jagah team kii kaman sambhaal rahe the
 He became a victim of Smith's steak shot
 salaami ballebaaj murali vijay (21) ne stuart binni par chakka jadaa lekin vah us samay bhaagyashaalee rahe jab praveen tambe kii gend par karun nair ne unka kaich tapakaa diya
 Vijay then hit a six over Maurice but he was run out and returned to the pavilion
 toornament main pehla match khel rahe marsh ne is bich kuch aakshark shot khele
 After hitting fours on binny and copper, he also hit two fours on Rahul Tewatia
 maxwell (01) haalanki ek baar phir naakaam rahe or leg spinner tevatiya kii gend par deep midwicket par smith ko kaich de baithe jisase punjab kaa score teen wicket par 59 ran ho gaya
 Marsh completed a 32-ball half-century with two sixes over Tewatia
 miller ne watasan par chakke ke saath 13wein over main team ke ranon kaa shatak puraa kiya
 Marsh, however, caught Rahane on long on in an attempt to hit a six on copper, ending his 58-run stormy partnership with Miller
 marsh ne 40 gend kaa saamana karte hue paanch chauke or teen chakke maare
 Punjab needed 72 runs to win in the last five overs
 miller ne foconor par lagaataar do chhakkon ke saath ran gati badhaai
 Wriddhiman Saha (19 runs off 8 balls) also hit three fours on Maurice but was bowled by missing this fast bowler's straight ball
 miller ne hooda par do chhakkon ke saath 29 gend main 50 ran puure kiye lekin agali gend par binni ko kaich de baithe
 He hit a four and a five sixes in his 30-ball innings
 isse pehle rahane ne captain watasan ke saath pehle wicket ke liye 95 ran jodakar team ke majboot score kii neenv rakhi
 He made just 3 for the second wicket with Deepak Hooda (19)
 3 over main 41 ran bhi jode
 Rahane, an orange cap holder, appeared in rhythm from the beginning
